Sports News

Hubei Defeats Shanghai in the First Game of the Far East Basketball Preliminary Round, Making a Stunning Impression. 39-43 Renowned Players from the Hubei Team Display Extraordinary Skills. The Shanghai Team's Carelessness on the Court Led to a Big Mistake. Tonight at 8 PM: Nanjing vs. Shanghai. 185

Shanghai vs. Hubei in the first game of the Far East basketball preliminary round took place at 8 PM last night at the baseball field's open-air court. There were 300-400 spectators. Shanghai's initial ten minutes of slackness led to a situation that was hard to turn around. Later line-up changes attempted to develop the game, and although they briefly surpassed with a score of 29-27 in the second half, they ultimately lost 39-43 in a miserable defeat. Hubei's outstanding talent and tight formation made their victory over Shanghai not accidental. Tonight at 8 PM, Shanghai will compete against Nanjing.

The two teams' strengths: Shanghai's guards did not seem to exert their full effort. Lu and Sun both had merits and demerits. Forwards Qian and Feng were too impatient and repeatedly missed opportunities. Chen Xianglong was extremely steady, accumulating points and performing the best. Hubei's Wu Guolin's defense was especially effective. Chen Shengkui was as brave as ever, serving as a cornerstone of the team. Yu Jingxiao lived up to his name as the only center talent. Ge Ke was also not weak. Wang Jianming worked very hard. The entire team had sufficient strength and coordinated well, unlike Shanghai, which was flustered and disorganized.

Disorganized Line-up: Shanghai initially started with Hu Zhengqu, Zhou Dayun, Qiu Guangxie, Chen Zongqi, and Zhang Jinxiang, but they were at a loss. Although the opponent repeatedly fouled, they all missed the opportunities. The score went from 2-10 to 5-16, and the situation was precarious. The five players were completely replaced to reorganize. Chen Xianglong repeatedly contributed, while Hubei continued to flourish. The first half ended with a score of 15-25, with Shanghai at a disadvantage.

Shanghai Surpassed: During the break, several gasoline lamps were extinguished and two were broken by the ball. Replacements were made, delaying the start by five minutes. However, due to the lack of four lamps, the light was dimmer. Shanghai tried to counterattack with great momentum. Chen Xianglong scored three consecutive times, and Sun Baoqing responded with two, scoring a total of ten points, making the score a tie at 25-25. It was thought that Shanghai had a chance to turn things around. Before long, Hubei's Ge Ke scored, taking the lead again with a score of 27-25. Shanghai continued its efforts, and Sun and Chen made further contributions, taking the lead with a score of 29-27.

Ultimately Defeated: At this point, the Shanghai team seemed to have the hope of directly attacking the enemy's stronghold. Who knew that after a short standoff, Ge Ke scored again, making it a tie again. Wu and Chen scored twice, making it 31-29, with the Shanghai team still succumbing. Later, the score became 32-32 and 34-34. Unexpectedly, from then on,

The Shanghai team repeatedly missed opportunities, and the match became more intense. The Shanghai team's forwards were sloppy, and Hubei took the opportunity to rise, with Chen Shengkui and Ge Ke scoring successively, soaring to 41-34. The Shanghai team made a final struggle, making it 38-41, but ultimately time ran out, making it impossible to recover, and they narrowly lost 39-43. The referees were Jin Zhaojun and Wu Jiatang.

Participation in the Far Eastern Games Preliminary Track and Field Trials Completed; Four New National Records Created - Shot Put, Discus, Javelin, 10,000 Meters - Rain and Cold Weather Affected Other Results 186

Our country's preliminary track and field trials for the 10th Far Eastern Games were completed yesterday afternoon, resulting in four new national records: (1) Chen Baoqiu, shot put, 12.655 meters; (2) Leng Peigen, discus, 37.85 meters; (3) Peng Yongxin, javelin, 48.92 meters; (4) Sun Che, 10,000 meters, 34 minutes 49 seconds. Other results were either affected by the cold spring weather, the small number of participants reducing the competitive interest, or the loose and wet ground after the rain, resulting in mediocre performances that were disappointing. It is hoped that after the association makes its selections, they will practice diligently and make rapid progress. The preliminary results are as follows:

Quick Notes on the Preliminary Track Events 189

(100 Meters) Only five participants, Liu Changchun, who was closely watched, stood aside. Although he registered, he did not participate, reportedly to focus on the 200 meters. Others such as Wang Jihuai, Xu Biao, and Hao Chunde also did not participate. The race started after the second gunshot. The situation was very even. A difference only became apparent at 60 meters, with Cheng Jinguan and Zhao Bingheng slightly ahead. At the finish line, Zhao trailed Cheng Jinguan by a shoulder. Han Jinglin came in third. Gu Zaiping was also very close to Han. Su Xiaoru, whose foot had not fully recovered, came in last. Cheng's time of 11 seconds was good. Zhao's was 11.1 seconds.

(200 Meters) Liu Changchun took to the field for the 200 meters, showcasing his skills, as it is his specialty. Only four people participated. Cheng Jinguan and Wang Jihuai did not participate. Liu took the lead within 40 meters of the start and led all the way to the end. Zhao Bingheng and Han Jinglin competed fiercely. At the finish line, Liu was five meters ahead of Han, and Han beat Zhao by a shoulder, avenging his loss in the 100 meters. Liu's time of 22.7 seconds was not outstanding.

(400 Meters) Only four participants, but although the national record was not broken, the competition was more exciting. Dong Shuzhao gave up the 800 meters to focus on this event. He indeed prevailed with 53.9 seconds over Zeng Rongzhong, a good result. Dong led all the way, and Zeng chased closely behind at 300 meters. However, at the finish line, Zeng was still six meters behind Dong. Zeng's time of 54.8 seconds was his usual performance. Li Yanxiang was third with 55.5 seconds.

(800 Meters) Four participants. With Dong Shuzhao's withdrawal, Luo Qinglong had no opponent. He led all the way. Jia Lianren and Li Yanxiang fought fiercely. At 600 meters, Jia surged ahead of Li. After another 50 meters, Li was in front of Jia. After another 50 meters, Li fell behind Jia again. From then on, Jia remained in second place. Luo was six meters ahead of Jia, and Li was three meters behind Jia. Luo's time of 2 minutes 6.7 seconds was mediocre. (1,500 Meters) Another competition of four people. Zheng Sen took the lead from the start, followed by Hou Dechong, Dong Jiaxie, and Yin Zongchen. Zheng was still in the lead at 400 meters and 800 meters, followed by Hou. Yin Zongchen had already surpassed Dong, but they were closely packed, with very little difference. At 1,200 meters, Yin Zongchen surpassed Hou Dechong. In the last 300 meters, Yin sprinted up, overtaking Zheng Sen and finishing first by six meters. The time of 4 minutes 6.7 seconds was very disappointing.

(High Hurdles) Liu Xiangjun, Chen Jiayou, and Chen Guojun competed. One second after the starting gun, Liu suddenly stopped and returned to the starting point. The starter, Jiang Xiangqing, saw this and fired a second gun, calling back the two Chens to rerun. As a result of the rerun, Liu Yingjun finished first with 17 seconds, but knocked down one hurdle. Chen Jiayou knocked down two hurdles, while Chen Guojun did not jump over a single hurdle, resulting in his score being canceled, an unexpected poor performance. (Hurdles) Wang Jingxi arrived late and competed against Tao Yingjie. They advanced side by side, with the difference only becoming apparent after 200 meters. At this point, Wang Jingxi knocked down a hurdle, and Tao seized the opportunity to take the lead. Tao was three meters ahead of Wang, with a time of 60 seconds, showing no improvement.

The 10,000 Meters is Highly Interesting, Sun Che's Skills are Exceptional - Time of 34 Minutes 49 Seconds - Top Three All Set New Records - Shanxi Athletes are Very Popular 190

The 10,000-meter race attracted the most attention. The bald-headed long-distance runners from Shanxi were welcomed by the audience. Sun Che, who recently set a new record of 34 minutes 1 second in Tianjin, and Gu Desheng, Wang Zhenglin, and Jin Zhongkang, who were involved in disputes at the National Games, were all present. Even a rickshaw puller participated, but dropped out halfway. In reality, there were only six runners. Gu Desheng also dropped out at 8,000 meters, so only five people finished. As a result, Sun Che indeed broke the national record with a time of 34 minutes 49 seconds, overwhelming the others.

(Sun Che Finished First) Sun Che remained in first place from the first lap to the 25th lap. The greatest distance was at 8,000 meters, when he was 60 meters ahead of Chen Shusen and over 400 meters ahead of Jin Zhongkang. At the finish line, he showed no signs of fatigue, which was truly remarkable. The second-place finisher, Chen Shusen, also remained in second place throughout the race. His sprint in the final lap was impressive, catching up from 40 meters to finish only three meters behind Sun Che. Chen's time of 34 minutes 51.8 seconds also broke the national record.

(Wang Zhenglin Made Great Progress) Wang Zhenglin's third-place finish, with a time of 35 minutes 10.8 seconds, also broke the national record, showing commendable progress. He closely followed Li Denggui throughout the race. At 8,000 meters, he suddenly surged ahead, overtaking Li and taking the lead. However, in the final 1,000 meters, Li regained the lead, but Wang eventually pulled ahead again by a distance of ten meters to finish third. Jin Zhongkang, although lagging behind by 400 meters, still finished the entire race.

(5) Chen Baoqiu Sets New National Record in Shot Put (Photo by Ye Changlie)

Overview of Field Event Competitions 191

(New Shot Put Record) Chen Baoqiu confidently took the crown, as was expected. His usual results had exceeded 13 meters, so there were high hopes for him to achieve that goal. However, try after try, he was unsuccessful. Fortunately, on his fourth attempt, he surpassed the 12-meter mark, reaching a new national record of 12.655 meters, surpassing the 12.55 meters at the White Rainbow Games. This was satisfactory. Liu Renxiu's first attempt was 12.335 meters, also a new record, but he showed no further improvement. The big man, Liu Furun, was third with 12.05 meters. Yang Yongcan was fourth, failing to reach the 12-meter mark. Cheng Bichun's result was less than 10 meters, and it was a bit overconfident of him to participate in the preliminary trials.

(New Discus Record) Leng Peigen had a good result of 37.64 at the White Rainbow Games. Yesterday, with the competition from Zhang Lingjia and Liu Jingren, he was particularly careful. His first two attempts were not satisfactory. On his third throw, he achieved his goal, reaching 37.85 meters, surpassing Liu Renxiu's national record of 36.50 meters, and it was against the wind. Zhang Lingjia was third with 36.02 meters, and Cheng Bichun was fourth with 32.40 meters, which was mediocre.

(Very Satisfied with the Javelin) Peng Yongxin's javelin skills have long been famous in the country. After setting a new national record of 48.92 meters at last year's National Games, he broke his own record with over 50 meters in the North China preliminary trials. Yesterday, despite facing headwinds, he was still able to maintain his usual skills, achieving 49.23 meters, which was not easy. Tang Xianzhou was second with 46.12 meters, which was also not bad. Pan Chengbin was third with 44.71 meters, which was far worse than the 48.24 he achieved in the pentathlon at his school's sports meet, indicating that he was still not confident. Hao Chunde was fourth with 43.80.

(Great Disappointment in the High Jump) Gu or Wang Shilin and Wu Bixian had all cleared 1 meter 80 in the past, but they have regressed significantly recently. Gu has been out of practice for a long time, and Wang Shilin recently equaled the national record with 1.82 meters at the North China preliminary trials, but he was very disappointing yesterday. No one achieved much. In the end, Wang Shilin, Wu Bixian, Gu or Ge Ke, and Liu Mingru were the last five, competing for the height of 1.75 meters. Only Wu Bixian cleared it, while the others failed. The cold weather and piercing wind certainly had a significant impact.

(Significant Regression in the Long Jump) Before the jump, the 6.91-meter mark was measured to motivate the competitors. Everyone was dispirited and unsuccessful, with significant regression. Wang Jihuai achieved 6.485 meters on his third jump, securing his victory. Hao Chunde jumped 6.30 meters on his third jump. Lu Yaxiong jumped 6.43 meters on his final jump, surpassing Hao and finishing second. Zhang Jiakui was fourth with 6.205.

(Pole Vault in Poor Condition) Only Fu Baolu, Wang He, and Huang Yi participated. Fu's first place was not in question, but his results regressed significantly. Huang Yi failed at 3.26 meters. Wang He was eliminated at 3.33 meters. Fu Baolu cleared 3.51 meters and then attempted 3.66 meters four times, but was unsuccessful.

(Triple Jump Obstructed) The triple jump was the last event in the track and field competition. At that time, the audience surged into the field, surrounding the jumping pit, making it impossible to hold the event properly. The audience's lack of order was deplorable, and the lack of prior preparation of the venue was also regrettable. As a result, the results were greatly affected, and the event was hastily concluded. Situ Guang achieved 13.41 on his second jump. Yang Daogui achieved 13.66 on his sixth jump, surpassing Situ to win the championship. Zhang Jiakui was third with 13.05, and Lu Yaxiong was fourth with 12.49.

Manchukuo's Participation in the Far East Games is Hopeless - The Philippines Responds that Japan Must First Revise the Charter - Japan Argues that the Philippines is Adhering to the Rules 194

The Philippines Replied that the Charter Must First Be Revised (National News Agency, Manila, 13th) The Philippine Amateur Athletic Federation issued a reply to Japan today, stating that the Philippine side is acting entirely in the spirit of sportsmanship, without any other purpose. The Association pointed out that the Philippines has already expressed approval for Manchukuo's participation and hopes that Japan's wishes to help Manchukuo can be realized based on the Far East Charter passed in Tokyo in 1930. However, this proposal must be agreed upon by all members, and China has expressed opposition, so the realization of this matter is impossible. We sincerely hope that the Japanese Sports Association will recognize the legislative position and make it impossible to resolve Manchukuo's participation in accordance with the charter. If Japan hopes to revise the charter at this general assembly, the Philippines is willing to consider this proposal in detail. Everything will be based on the most friendly spirit and the attitude of sportsmen.

Deciding Attitude After the Philippines' Reply 195

(Dentsu, Tokyo, 14th) The Far East Games issue is still in critical condition. The Japan Athletic Association is making every effort. The Philippine Islands held an executive committee this morning and decided on a reply to Japan. Its reply is expected to reach Japan this evening. Future developments will depend on the content of the reply. The Association will hold a full meeting tonight to discuss and determine its final attitude. However, since it will be consulting with Dr. Yamamoto and Kazutsuru Matsuzawa, the final decision may be made on the night of the 15th, but depending on the content of the Philippine Islands' reply, it is also possible that it will decide not to participate in the Games.

Yamamoto Says it is Too Early to Withdraw from the Games 196

(Dentsu Agency, Nagasaki, 14th) Dr. Tadahiko Yamamoto and Kazutsuru Matsuzawa, who returned to Japan from Shanghai, arrived here at 2:00 PM today aboard the Nagasaki Maru and left for Tokyo by train at 2:40 PM. Dr. Yamamoto spoke to reporters as follows: It seems not impossible for Manchukuo to participate in the Far East Games as a guest. It is too early to say that the attitude of the Philippine Islands is completely hopeless. Some are advocating withdrawal and the organization of another Games, but now is not the time. After I arrive in Tokyo, I will carefully consult on the matter.

Manchukuo's Participation in the Far Eastern Games is Hopeless 197

(Hualian News Agency, Nagasaki, 14th) Yamamoto and Matsuda, the two representatives who went to Manila via Shanghai last month to attend the Far East Games roundtable conference, and Kanda, the representative of Manchukuo, arrived here at 2:20 PM this afternoon aboard the Nagasaki Maru. Representative Yamamoto told reporters, "Manchukuo's" participation in the Far East Games seems hopeless. The Philippines is too attached to the rules, and there is no hope of changing their attitude. As for the idea of ​​holding joint competitions between Japan and "Manchukuo" (i.e., joint athletic games), it seems too early. Yamamoto and others will take the express train to the Northeast at 2:40 PM.

Women's World, Issue 9

A Critique of Two Views on Love: Biyun 210

— Biyun

When we talk about "love," people immediately feel a sense of sweetness, as if it contains endless allure. But, is this allure, this sweetness, detached from everything else? Is it the primary purpose of life? Then our poets and artists, all those who uphold the supreme importance of love, will smile and answer: Yes! There is no life without love; love is supreme, divine.

However, unfortunately, being immersed in the sea of love all day long, subsisting only on kisses without eating anything else, cannot withstand the hunger in one's stomach. Without food to eat, without a house to live in, even without clothes to wear, the god of love, "Venus," will not grace you with its presence. Thus, so-called "divine love" cannot transcend the material necessities upon which human survival depends. In other words, even those who say "love is purely spiritual" cannot live on love alone while starving!

Moreover, love is also subject to the limitations of time and space. In feudal societies, women were bound by the "three obediences and four virtues," and there was no talk of love at all; they were merely slaves of men, or rather, more accurately, slaves of society. Even if a few women at that time were able to savor the "taste of love," it was not the result of their own pursuit, but rather a stroke of unfathomable luck under the dictates of "parents' orders and matchmakers' words." By the time of so-called "civilized society" in modern times, the situation is different. Men and women can freely choose their partners, and on the surface, they seem to be free from any restrictions. Thus, various theories such as "free love" and "the divinity of love" have become a temporary fashion of this era. However, in reality, although love at this time is not bound by etiquette, it is dictated by money. "With money, you can make the devil push the millstone," and "love" at this time can also be bought with money. Don't you see wealthy old men in their forties and fifties talking about "free love" with school queens in their teens? Don't you see thousands upon thousands of young women selling their bodies and souls to many strangers every night? This is the factual manifestation of how so-called divine love is subject to the control of money. If women were slaves in feudal societies, then women, and even the majority of men, in so-called civilized societies in modern times are commodities that can be bought and sold. The so-called "free love" and "divinity of love" here are simply self-deceiving lies!

Since love is subject to the limitations of human life and the constraints of time and space, the primary purpose of life is not love, but the struggle for survival. Without survival, there is nothing, and therefore there is no talk of love. Those who are oppressed by life's pressures will inevitably suffer from pain, and the so-called "enjoyment of love" will be out of the question. Therefore, the meaning of life in the present society lies in striving for liberation and progress in life. This meaning is especially important when the majority of people are subjected to the cruel oppression of life.

However, here comes another strange opinion, and this opinion comes from many new young men and women: the "purely sexualist" view that completely denies the function of human emotions.

Some modern young men and women, in opposing the supremacy of love, believe that the relationship between the sexes is nothing more than "sexual desire." Thus, they vent their sexual desire here today and steal affections there tomorrow. These are simply superficial materialists who have lost their minds and emotions, simpletons who do not understand what "love" is.

Of course, love cannot exist independently without a sexual relationship, but we cannot therefore completely deny it. Prostitutes are constantly venting their lust, but they are often in a sea of ​​misery and have no love. A couple with a bad relationship, although they sometimes have sexual relations, the fact of divorce is very common because there is no strong affection between them. These facts shatter the views of those sexualists who completely deny love!

If those who uphold the supremacy of love consider love to be the primary purpose of life, then extreme sexualists, in their desperate pursuit of sexual satisfaction, will also abandon the true meaning of life and live solely to satisfy their sexual lives. Both are unique to people in the present society who feel that everything is meaningless and the future is bleak. Here, the extreme left (purely sexualist) and extreme right (supremacy of love) opinions on the issue of love converge on different paths.

While poets and artists who generally sing the praises of the supremacy of love are ridiculous, the new young men and women who advocate pure sexualism are even more proof of their immaturity and ignorance. They believe that they are thoroughly opposing the decadent and decadent views of love of the petty bourgeoisie, but they do not realize that they are unknowingly embarking on the path of decadence and decadence themselves.

Of course, we are not ascetics and do not oppose young men and women from talking about love; not at all. We believe:

First, love is not supreme, but is subject to the limitations of human life, times, and society.

Second, love is not inferior, merely a means of venting sexual desire; we have never completely denied the role of emotions in love.

Third, love is not only a combination of sex and emotion, but also a combination of life. Our love must be built on a foundation of mutual understanding, mutual encouragement, and consistency in thought and action. Moreover, in life, we must constantly strive to improve human life and promote the work of social evolution.

Finally, we must not regard love as sacred and live for love, nor should we treat love as a game to be played with at will. These are all manifestations of decadence and decadence, and they hinder the progress of humanity.

Hygiene During Pregnancy 211

— Physician Shen Jian'an

Pregnancy is a physiological phenomenon, not a disease. However, during pregnancy, the nutrients ingested by the mother must also be supplied to the fetus, so the resistance of various parts of the body is very weak. On the one hand, she suffers from inevitable physiological symptoms, such as headaches, weakness, loss of appetite, etc., which make the body very weak. At that time, if affected by an accidental illness, it will have a great impact on the health and life of both mother and child. Therefore, the suffering of ten months of pregnancy also becomes the bond that binds mother and child together like their lives! Especially in Chinese society, where general medical knowledge is not widespread, the three matters of pregnancy and childbirth seem to be hovering on the crossroads of life and death. Therefore, many women with some knowledge but not thoroughly understand the process are averse to pregnancy, and even avoid marriage. This is not an optimistic phenomenon for society and the nation. But is pregnancy ultimately dangerous? Painful? Certainly not. This is a natural physiological phenomenon. As long as we pay a little attention during pregnancy, that is, if we obtain the way of hygiene, then pregnancy is not dangerous at all and will not be painful at all. Therefore, the method of hygiene during pregnancy is something that everyone should understand, so as to create a healthy and happy mother's body and future little citizens! Now I will explain the simplest and most important points one by one for women to refer to!

Exercise

Violent exercise should be absolutely prohibited. Normally, one should seek physical tranquility, but one should not lie in bed all day long. It is best to do appropriate gentle exercises, often inhale fresh air, take walks outdoors, get more sunlight, so as to refresh the mind, and do less of the usual strenuous housework. Long-distance travel, mountain climbing, going upstairs, dancing, horseback riding, cycling, carrying or lifting heavy objects, etc. must be absolutely prohibited. Even prolonged sitting, playing cards, kneeling, washing, etc. are harmful and useless to the mother's body.

Food and Drink

Although it is not necessary to completely break the habits of the past, it is best to appropriately ingest nutritious, rich, and easily digestible things. All foods with too much fat, and things that easily produce gas in the intestines, and stimulating foods (such as peppers, chili peppers, eggplants, shochu, tobacco, etc.) should not be overeaten. However, a small amount of wine, weak tea, or coffee can increase the benefits for both the mother's body and the fetus.

Clothing

Clothes should be clean, loose, and comfortable. The chest and lower abdomen should not be tightly bound. The climate should be kept at an appropriate temperature, and should not be too hot or too cold. A belly band should be tied around the abdomen, with the purpose of maintaining the fetus's body temperature and fixing the position of the fetus. After wrapping the abdomen, the abdomen will not fall downwards, and the fetus will not be too large, making childbirth easier. In our country, it has always been thought that belly bands are harmful and useless. This is not right. Also, some women have always had the habit of tightly binding the chest and waist, so the abdomen is compressed and blood circulation is obstructed. As a result, facial swelling, lower limb varicose veins, etc. occur, and the health and development of the fetus are hindered. Special attention must be paid to these during pregnancy.

Bowel Movements

Pregnant women are most prone to constipation. After harmful gases in the intestines, it can cause various systemic symptoms, such as nausea, vomiting, hemorrhoids, gastrointestinal diseases, etc. To prevent constipation, one must perform appropriate gentle exercises every day, eat fruit after meals, or drink a cup of cold boiled water or cold milk on an empty stomach in the morning. It is necessary to make her have a bowel movement at a certain time, succeeding in creating a natural habit. If there is no bowel movement for two days, one must ask a doctor to use soapy water enema or glycerin enema, or internal use of (MagSulfi50) fifteen grams of Epsom salt. However, general drastic purgatives sold in pharmacies often induce the disadvantages of premature birth or miscarriage, so they must be absolutely prohibited (if you have a disease during pregnancy, you must not take quinine pills, because quinine pills have the possibility of causing miscarriage for pregnant women.

Urination

In the early stages of pregnancy, you must not often keep urine in your bladder. When you have urine, you should excrete it, otherwise it will cause retroversion or retroflexion of the uterus, and sometimes proteinuria and diabetes may occur. It is best to often ask a doctor to check for the presence of protein or sugar, which can prevent diabetes or nephritis.

Mental State

The mental state of the mother's body will affect the fetus. This is called prenatal education. After the pregnant woman's spirit is adversely affected, health disorders occur, and in severe cases, miscarriage can occur. Therefore, pregnant women should often be quiet and recuperate, and should not often talk to pregnant women about difficult births, miscarriages, and all kinds of difficult news about first births, or strange stories about deformed fetuses, so as not to cause pregnant women to be frightened and affect the fetus. Pregnant women should not read novels, pictures, dramas, movies, etc. with strong stimuli, or excessive joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness. The nerves should not be overworked, sleep must be sufficient, and a safe life must be had.

Body Cleanliness

After conception, there is often excessive secretion from the external genitalia, causing vulvitis or transmission of other diseases, so it must be washed with lukewarm water every day, and a bath must be taken once every two days. However, too hot or long-term bathing can cause termination of pregnancy. When washing, water should not be washed into the vagina, unless there is a vaginal lesion, can vaginal washing be performed! This vaginal washing has specialized equipment, so you must consult a doctor.

Breasts

The breast area must be liberated. It should not be tightly bound. In the last month of pregnancy, wash with clean water or alcohol to increase the resistance of the skin on the nipple area and prevent nipple cracks or transmission. If the nipple is underdeveloped or sunken, lift the nipple several times a day to gradually protrude the nipple, so that the baby will not feel difficult when breastfeeding after childbirth and the nipple will not hurt.

Sexual Intercourse

If you are sure that you are pregnant, sexual intercourse must be limited, otherwise it is often easy to transmit infections. Normally, after four months of pregnancy, sexual intercourse must be absolutely prohibited!

The Views of Great Thinkers of the World on the Woman Question (2) 213

— Hua

Two: Marie Gouze

Marie Gouze, whom we mentioned in our previous article on Condorcet, was one of the first women in the French Revolution to participate in political activities and organize the women's rights movement. She was born in Montauban in southern France, some say in 1753, others say in 1755. Her mother was either a dressmaker or a poor woman who picked up rags. Her father's background is unknown.

Marie Gouze was a lecturer. At that time, she often attended and lectured at women's group meetings, public gatherings, and the clubs of various political parties. She also attended and lectured at the French National Assembly after the revolution. At that time, the National Assembly allowed women to submit proposals and express opinions before discussing the issues listed on the agenda. Marie Gouze's enthusiastic and beautiful words, her clever arguments, and her gentle ideas repeatedly moved the national representatives. She changed the status quo by means of publishing pamphlets, writing essays, and issuing declarations.

Marie Gouze's activities can be mainly said to be a deep concern for the improvement of women's own status. She believed that the root of all evils was in men controlling women; she believed that the only way for women to reach the highest stage of human development was through freedom and women's rights. To obtain freedom and women's rights, the only way is to use the united strength of the oppressed. To encourage and unite women with wise and righteous demands, and to lead them to fight for women's true rights, this was Marie Gouze's basic goal of exhausting her talents and working hard. She said on a small "Women's Rights" leaflet:

"Men! Who gave you the right to oppress women? Please take a look at the entire natural world; is there anything in it that resembles your arbitrariness and violence? Try to look at living matter, ask the beasts, study the plants, investigate, explore, and analyze all the relationships between the sexes in nature; everywhere they are loving each other, everywhere there is the eternal, ingenious, innate harmony and unity of all things. You have just eliminated the privileges of the nobility, please also abolish the privileges of men! People are beginning to enjoy their rights, and black slaves are also being liberated. Why not liberate women?"

Marie Gouze tried her best to teach her own sisters to learn the cause of liberation. She said to them:

"Has the revolutionary era not yet arrived for us women? Should we live in solitude for all ages, and never actively participate in social construction?"

The famous "Declaration of the Rights of Man" during the French Revolution only explained the rights of men unilaterally, and did not mention women in a single word. Marie Gouze, in response to it, specifically issued a declaration that was almost equally famous: "Declaration of the Rights of Woman." She clearly, thoroughly, and movingly put forward the demand for complete equality for women in society and in politics. The full text of the declaration is translated on the left:

"Women are born free, with rights equal to those of men. The purpose of every good society is to protect the rights of both sexes, which cannot be deprived by any law; freedom, progress, security, and sanctions against oppression. ... But in fact, the rights of women endowed by nature have only been recognized within a narrow range so far. The nation upon which the state is built is composed of men and women, and the legal system should be an expression of the will of this society. All female citizens, just like all male citizens, should participate in self-government, individually or through representatives they elect. Self-government should be equal for all people. Therefore, all male and female citizens, according to their abilities, must be allowed to hold all social positions, powers, and duties; only the difference in their virtue and talent can be used as a standard for election. Women have the right to mount the rostrum, and they have the right to mount the lecture platform; they must enjoy both of these rights. However, women's rights should serve the common happiness, and should not serve the interests of sex.

Women, like men, should share the national currency; likewise, women, like men, have the right to demand that national treasury management be public. If the basic law of the country? When it is not formulated by the majority of the people who constitute the nation, it will definitely be invalid. Women, please try it... The torch of truth has already dispelled the black clouds of stupidity and tyranny; when will you regain your sight? Unite and use the power of reason and justice to resist brute force! You will soon see that men will no longer painfully pursue you, they will proudly raise their heads, puff out their chests, and share with you the rights of mankind for all ages, and advance hand in hand with you."

In short, Marie Gouze, in her leaflets, in her pamphlets, in her lectures, in political party clubs and academic groups, was everywhere excitedly arguing about the issue of women's rights. She founded the first magazine in history to promote the women's movement. At that time, the French National Assembly received countless petitions in favor of and against women's equality. Marie Gouze believed that the time had come to establish political organizations to unite women, so she founded her Women's Political Association and served as their leader and propagandist.

However, although Marie Gouze's words were ingenious and moving, her remarks on the woman question were still scattered and disorganized. She completely blamed men for the responsibility of existing social relations (which were formed due to economic necessity), believing that this was due to men's shortsightedness and selfishness, and neglected the background of social economics. This is something that should be paid attention to.

What I Have Seen of European Women 214

— Yang

This was already three years ago. When we arrived in England, France, Germany, Belgium, Switzerland, etc., we generally did not stay in hotels due to time and savings, economic relations. Instead, we rented houses and stayed in boarding houses (pensions), which are a type of apartment-style residence that provides room and board. There were many opportunities to get close to their families, so their lives were clearer.

Housewives: Although the standard of living in China has been increasing in recent years, it is still far different compared to European countries! Because people in China are cheap, it is very common for ordinary families to employ two or three servants. For example, in France, hiring a female worker costs five francs per hour; in Germany, it is about one mark (approximately one national currency). This type of female worker is almost a specialized profession. They attend school-like classes and can enter and exit many homes every day according to the hour. Therefore, being a housewife is busy from morning to night! The husband goes out to work early; they quickly send the older children to school; feed the younger children milk; wipe the furniture, sweep the floor and windows; and then push the children's strollers to the vegetable market to select the day's vegetables. Returning home, they take off their outer clothes, put on aprons, and cook food very carefully and hurriedly. They can't bear to waste five centimes (copper coins), let alone spend five francs to hire a female worker to take over for an hour. Especially on Saturdays, that is their big cleaning day, they should wash all the utensils. On that day, we can see old and young women flushing the gates and stairs with tap water and scrubbing hard with rough brushes. Only Sunday is their most leisurely and happy day. The family wears neat clothes; they go to the suburbs or parks to absorb fresh air; or visit museums and art galleries; of course, movie theaters, dance halls, and cafes also have their footprints; this is how they dispel the fatigue of the past six days!

Women in society: There are very many European women working outside. Female staff account for almost 80-90% of large companies, shops, and small schools. Girls must go out to earn a living and become independent at the age of seventeen or eighteen. However, their salaries are very low, with monthly incomes of only two or three hundred francs, or up to five hundred francs at most. They eat simply and save money slowly because they are not yet married! When a partner is selected, he will first ask her how much dowry she has, because she is responsible for everything needed for the two to form a family, such as tables, chairs, beds, bedding, and kitchen utensils; as for the subsequent life, he will be responsible for it. Women with ugly faces are very difficult to find a spouse! Or, if they marry the wrong person, once they get married, he will cheat her out of years of hard-earned savings and abandon her, which is even more pitiful! In addition, after the European war, countless men died or were disabled, and there were more women than men in society, so many of them would rather live alone. With the above-mentioned difficulties, most European women have married people of color from the East in recent years, especially our China. The students studying abroad are mostly young masters from the propertied class, who return home after completing their studies (?) and act as some committee member, some leader, or become university professors. Wouldn't they immediately enjoy happiness and become rich wives? Who would be willing to do the job of sweeping and cooking again! Of course, there are also those who do not change their original thrifty ways, which depends on the individual's environment!

Miss Clogs and the Black Prince's Engagement Suddenly Breaks Down 215

— Xuan

Doing or not doing the Imperial Concubine is a small matter

Doing or not doing a Beauty Trap is a big matter

Two months ago, Japanese newspapers extensively reported that an Ethiopian prince from Africa, due to his admiration for Japanese women, was selecting a bride in Japan. For a time, there were many applicants. As a result, Masako Kuroda, the daughter of Viscount Kuroda, was selected, which was widely regarded as a beautiful story throughout the country, keeping news reporters and magazine editors busy. Recently, Masako has been busy preparing for the wedding day and night, when suddenly the Ethiopian ambassador to Italy said that the international marriage of the black prince would be dissolved due to strong interference from a certain country.

When the news came, it naturally made the island nation people, who never forgot overseas development, feel greatly disappointed. Miss Masako was, of course, even more embarrassed. When she first received this news, she was said to be very excited and not very convinced. Finally, she said calmly: "Even if the engagement is really dissolved, I will not be depressed because of this. At least my actions this time have made Japanese women realize that Japanese women should be active overseas... My personal affairs are small, but the fact that Japan is so internationally oppressed really needs to be considered. At the same time, my painstaking effort to marry a black man's wife should also be understood by the general public, so I can be very comforted..." These words are sufficient to represent the psychology of Japanese women.

A Female Clerk's Conversation 216

— Man Lun

One afternoon, I went with a friend to a large company to buy leather shoes. There, we happened to meet a naive and lively young female clerk. She very kindly and humbly brought us pairs of leather shoes to try on. My friend began to chat with her. She told us that she was a junior high school graduate from Yangzhou. Because there were many sisters in her family and her father had lost his job, their financial situation was extremely difficult. She heard that a large company in Shanghai was recruiting female clerks, so she resolutely applied and was fortunate enough to be hired. Now, her monthly salary is thirty yuan. She shares a small room with a companion, with each paying three yuan for rent and seven yuan for food. The remaining twenty yuan must be used to send fifteen yuan to her parents, leaving only five yuan for her own expenses, including making clothes. As she spoke, we forgot about buying leather shoes. She continued, saying that she had to be at the company by eight o'clock in the morning and couldn't leave until after eight o'clock in the evening. ...Since coming here a few months ago, she has only worked in her assigned section. Although the company is so large, she feels like she is in a prison. All day long, she has to spend her time there. It's obvious that the piercingly cold winter has passed, and the welcoming warmth of spring has arrived, but we have no chance to admire the lovely tender green and bright red flowers and grass, or the green willows dancing in the wind. By the time we stop work, the lights are already shining, and the most important thing is to go home and eat. So, although our living problems have been solved, our youth is passing by in such a dim way. She continued, saying that besides this kind of life, there is another thing that makes her feel annoyed, and that is the customers who come and go. The female customers don't cause any trouble, but those hateful, slick-haired men often use irrelevant words to flirt with us, getting entangled, and their intention is nothing more than teasing. When we have free time, we also like to read the newspaper, but many of the news and short articles in the newspaper often stimulate our nerves. We are daughters of good families. Being a clerk is something that men also do. We didn't expect those who write articles to use us as material for ridicule. A few days ago, there was a cartoon in a certain newspaper that was full of things insulting women. We female clerks are also among those being scolded. When we were in school, we heard the teacher say that people should support themselves, and many people advocate that women should be economically independent. Doesn't economic independence mean going out to find work? Being a clerk is not a dishonorable thing. Although the clothes we wear are a bit more fashionable, that is the boss's order. We eat his food, so we have to obey... Why don't they (referring to the writers) think from the beginning, and only satirize us pitiful people...?

She seemed to have forgotten that she was working as a clerk. We also forgot about buying leather shoes. Women are most easily moved by emotion, and we were just very sympathetic to her.

Suddenly, a bell rang on the neighboring table, giving her a miraculous reaction. She then picked up another pair of leather shoes.

"Miss, please try these on..."

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Effort 234

— Bao Yu

Little friends! Do you know the meaning of effort? Effort is using your strength to do what you should do.

Little friends! Have you heard the story of the tortoise and the hare race? The tortoise walked very slowly, but it was willing to work hard, so it won. The hare ran very fast, but it was unwilling to work hard and fell asleep on the way; as a result, it failed!

In school, don't you often see that some students do well in their studies, and some students don't? The reason is that one is willing to work hard, and the other is not. There are many people in the world who are like hares, starting out with great effort, but later becoming unwilling to work hard. They fail! There are also very few people who are able to keep working hard, so they succeed!

Little friends! If you are willing to move forward diligently like a tortoise, your future will be very promising.

Little friends! Don't you always hope that your studies will improve day by day? Don't you admire great people? I tell you, if you want to realize your hopes, you only need to work hard to move forward.

The Law of the Jungle 235

— Ren Wei

The law of the jungle, where the weak are prey to the strong, is a natural principle. Big fish eat small fish, which is an inevitable fact. There is nothing controversial about it.

A big fish was chasing a small fish in the river. The small fish said, "Don't be so cruel, I am your kin!" "Kin? Now there are only two paths to take: the first is that I eat you, and the second is that you eat me." The small fish sighed at the size of its own body and said, "Then, please eat me!"

But, little friends! Please don't be afraid. Adults will never eat children, because you have loving parents to protect you, and you have national armies to defend you. However, if you ever leave the embrace of your parents, or leave the borders of your country, you will never have the same happy life as you do now.

Little friends! Before you leave your parents or your country, you should quickly study hard and strengthen your physique; otherwise, if you encounter someone stronger, you will not be able to defeat them, and they will harm you.

A Proverb 236

— You Ji

Little friends, I will tell you a proverb, a very meaningful proverb.

It is a Western proverb, and that proverb says: "Nothing will fall into the mouth of a sleeping fox." Little friends, this is a very true statement. Think about it, a sleeping fox's mouth is always closed, right? Then, even if something falls from above, it will not fall into its mouth. Moreover, there is not necessarily anything falling from above. Even if something does fall from above, and the sleeping fox's mouth is open, how can it be certain that the thing will fall into its mouth? So the proverb says that nothing will fall into the mouth of a sleeping fox, and that is true.

But why is it said to be a meaningful proverb? Originally, that proverb contains a kind of lesson. That lesson is that lazy people will never get anything. You see, the sleeping fox is lazy, isn't it? How can it get something to fall into its mouth if it doesn't move?

Little friends, you must not be lazy, you must be diligent, you must be diligent in studying, you must be diligent in cleaning, and you must be diligent in all good things. If you are diligent, your knowledge will improve, your body will be healthy, and you will get endless happiness.

Small Experience 237

[Z] Jianfen

Broken Glass

Do you do bamboo carving in your school? When scraping off the "bamboo green" layer from the surface of the bamboo, isn't it easy to damage the blade if you use a knife? You can use "broken glass" to scrape it, using its sharp edge to scrape off the "bamboo green." It is not only faster but also smoother than scraping with a knife.

Waste Paper Torn from the Calendar

Isn't the back of the waste paper torn from the calendar still a blank sheet of paper? We can accumulate them page by page and bind them into a small "scratchpad," which can be used as a diary or as a draft book for Chinese, arithmetic, and various other subjects.

Wild Geese's Lament 238

— Shi Yusheng

Oh! Oh!

I can't bear the desolation and loneliness of the frontier;

I flap my wings,

And fly over the mountains.

Fly, fly, fly,

South to the motherland.

I don't want to be a slave of a conquered nation anymore!

Fly, fly, fly,

Never mind morning and evening,

Never mind hunger and thirst,

I scream with my throat,

To shatter the illusions of those who are complacent!

Two Children's Songs 239

— Zhang Nancun

On Sunday, Min'er's father took him to Shanghai City God Temple. There were many children's toys for sale. Min'er had heard his teacher say that Japanese children's toys had always sold very well. Min'er saw many toys for sale and couldn't tell if they were Japanese or Chinese, so he didn't want to buy any of them. Later, he saw foreign mice for sale in a bird shop. Those foreign mice were climbing on a merry-go-round in a glass cage. Min'er thought it was very fun and said to his father, "Should we buy one and take it home to play with?" His father smiled and said to him, "You said you wouldn't buy foreign goods, aren't these foreign mice foreign goods?" Min'er held his father's hand, pulled him away, and said, "I will absolutely not buy foreign goods. I don't want these foreign mice, let's go!" His father saw how patriotic he was and thought he was very cute, so he said, "Although they are called foreign mice, they are actually raised and sold by Chinese people, not imported goods. You can buy them. I was just joking, don't misunderstand." So he bought two foreign mice and a glass cage for the mice to climb on, and when he went back, he also bought a Chinese paper lantern.

In the evening, Min'er saw the foreign mice climbing on the merry-go-round, and also held the lighted lantern in his hand, he was so happy that he wrote a foreign mice song and a lantern song, and sang them happily. His two children's songs are written below.

Foreign Mice

Foreign mice, red eyes, climbing on the merry-go-round, their feet never stop. They eat white rice and also work, better than lazy and naughty students.

Light the Lantern

In the New Year, light the lantern. Light the lantern and let it shine brightly. The lantern leads me on a bright path, do not enter a wrong path and ruin your life.

Different Houses in the World 240

— He Gongchao

(1) British brick house, (2) House of the Bolivian natives of South America, built with mud and branches, (3) House of the Lapp people, built with grass and soil, (4) Mud house of the Cameroonians, (5) House of the Maori people (residents of New Zealand), with human heads and other pictures painted on the pillars, (6) Small house of North American Indians, covered with bark, straw mats, or animal skins on the pillars, (7) House of the Vietnamese, built on wooden piles, (8) House of the Australians, built with branches, (9) Japanese paper house, (10) Tree house of the Mindanao people, (11) Grass house of the Hoshars, (12) Snow house of the Eskimos, (13) Wooden house of Russian peasants.

The houses that various ethnic groups in the world live in, like the clothes they wear, also have great differences. Because of the different climates and building materials, the forms of their houses are also very different. For example, the houses of the Eskimos living in the Arctic are built with snow blocks because snow blocks are the easiest building materials for them to obtain in winter. Russian peasants use wood to build houses because they live near large forests. In places where floods often occur, houses are often built on wooden piles or trees to prevent floods. In tropical regions like Africa, most of the houses are built with grass or mud, because there is plenty of grass and mud in the tropics. But in culturally developed places, the residences of the residents are mostly built with bricks and stones, and not much with local materials, such as mud and grass. The more developed the culture, the more solid and exquisite the architecture of the residence, which is the universal rule of the world.

Why Late? 241

— Xue Fan

The bell had been ringing for a long time, and Xu Bingsheng hurried in from outside the door with his schoolbag in his arms. Xu Bingsheng's face was obviously full of panic.

"Why are you so late?" the teacher asked. "Because our dishes were not cooked well today," Xu Bingsheng replied.

"So you argued with your family because the dishes were not cooked well? And therefore you were late?"

Xu Bingsheng said calmly, "No! Because the dishes were not cooked well, I couldn't eat."

The teacher felt even more strange. "Since you couldn't eat, then you should have come earlier."

"Teacher! Don't you understand? Because I couldn't eat, I couldn't walk!"

The students looked at each other and laughed, and the teacher also laughed.

New Fables 242

— Yu Bailu

(1) Unity is Strength

Once upon a time, there was an old man who had five sons. They were not harmonious and fought every day. Although he repeatedly advised them, nothing worked. One day, he thought of a way. He took a bundle of chopsticks and asked them to break it in turn, but the chopsticks were so tightly bound that they couldn't be broken no matter how hard they tried. After a while, he unbound the chopsticks and gave them to them one by one to break. Then, they broke them easily. Therefore, he taught them, "My children, you must always grasp the strength of unity! If you can unite together, no enemy can harm you. At the same time, if you are scattered by fighting, then any enemy can harm you!"

(2) Virtue Will Receive Equal Reward

A thirsty ant went to a small spring to drink water, ran too fast, and was washed into the water by the spring. A flying dove saw it and felt sorry for it, so it held a leaf in its beak and put it next to it. It was rescued, climbed onto the leaf, and when the leaf flowed near the spring, it quietly climbed onto the shore again. Not long after, this dove was seen by a hunter in the forest. Just as he was aiming his gun at it, the ant happened to be next to the hunter's foot, so he quickly stung the hunter's foot. The hunter was hit in the dark, but the dove escaped.

Flying a Kite 243

— Ning Ziqiang

Little friends, in this warm and sunny weather, do you still remember the fun of flying kites? I think all of you little friends will not forget, and you will definitely remember to play this game on Sundays or holidays.

There are many kinds of kites: fish, birds, old men, centipedes, everything that should be here, not everything. They are called paper kites because someone installs a bowstring on them. The wind excites the string, so they are also called kites.

Little friends, do you also know the inventor of electricity, the American Benjamin Franklin? Originally, when he was taking the kite, there was thunder and rain in the sky. He used a copper key and hung it on the kite string. At the same time, he saw the key flashing brightly. So he felt that metal had the effect of inducing current, so he became an inventor in the electrical world.

Children's Corner

Sweet Buddha Shanghai Minsheng Primary School 244

— Xie Wan

Once upon a time, there was a man who sold honey. One day, he was carrying a load of honey to sell when he suddenly slipped and dropped the honey. He was very heartbroken, so he rolled around in the honey, getting honey all over his body. Because he was tired from rolling around, he fell asleep.

Many monkeys came and saw a person sleeping on the ground. They licked him with their tongues and found him very sweet. So they carried him home and treated him like a sweet Buddha, and they also brought many good things to offer him.

Later, the monkeys went out, and he woke up. Seeing so many things, he happily took them home and ate them.

Wang Er Catches Butterflies in the Campus

Oh, no, it's on the teacher's head

Animals' Self-Confidence 245

— Bing Yu

If little friends go to the zoo to play, when you come back, you will definitely have a kind of feeling, that is, which of the fierce and huge beasts has the strongest force? Which animal is the fiercest? Animals all have their own self-confident power. For example, when a lion encounters a strong member of the same species, it will show an angry face, perk up its spirits, tense its muscles, and reveal its sharp teeth, side by side, opening its jaws, showing a self-confident and fierce appearance. The lion is the king of beasts. With one swipe of its front limbs, cattle, deer, zebras, etc., will fall to the ground and die. "The vibration of its tail is an expression that it wants to kill people." Orangutans often fight crocodiles and large snakes in the forest or by the river. With its powerful arms, it can pull the crocodile's upper and lower jaws apart. It opens its mouth and bites the crocodile's throat to pieces. If the snake wraps around its body, it can bite the snake in the middle. The hippopotamus is the largest in the animal world. It is 15 feet long, weighs 4 tons, and is shaped like a barrel. Its mouth is wide and large. The boats that the natives hang are often swallowed by it, and even small ships can be dragged to the bottom of the water by it. The elephant is smaller than the hippopotamus. African giant elephants are up to 11.85 feet tall, and Indian elephants are also 10.5 feet tall. In ancient Rome, the elephant's great strength was often used for warfare. The natives of Ceylon ordered several elephants to work together to pull up trees that were 30 feet high and five feet in circumference. Its nose can break thick branches with a single curl. The African ape can kill a giant elephant with two fists. As for birds, the strongest is the ostrich, followed by the cassowary. Although these large birds cannot fly high, they walk faster than other winged birds. They use their long legs and sharp claws as weapons. If we are slapped by it, it will be difficult for us to survive.

A Rural Little Friend's Correspondence: Little Friends Seeking Wild Vegetables 246

— Ziming

Dear Little Friends;

Ah! How great is the authority of spring! Those melancholy and depressed willows, nourished by warm, soup-like sweet dew, caressed by a furnace-like sun, are actually dancing gracefully! The little birds, stretching their necks, sing melodious and clear songs, and many of us little friends greet them.

The wheat in the fields bows in welcome as a gentle breeze blows. The little grasses secretly reveal their tips, but the rapeseed smiles. Does it mark many crosses, or is it the spirit of Jesus?

Many little friends, in twos and threes, are searching for artemisia and alfalfa in the fields. One basket, two baskets, they take them home, and their parents smile. Sometimes they even take them to the market towns to sell, each basket for four or five copper coins. These little friends happily save up the money. It is a pity that they don't have the opportunity to go to school. But they often go to nearby schools to play on the slides, seesaws, and small swings...

Friends! We are people who have many opportunities to study. How can we relax? Let's work hard! Taking advantage of the bright and beautiful springtime.
